<span key="b9df7aaa0faf4bb9b8fdb64a647f00d4"><span offset-key="b9df7aaa0faf4bb9b8fdb64a647f00d4:0">Shows disk free space on file systems</span></span>

<span key="13a0926011f743adb8b6a0ec169e963e"><span offset-key="13a0926011f743adb8b6a0ec169e963e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="http://linuxcommand.org/lc3_man_pages/dir1.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a4385ec4f3f0412897505f15c151b96f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-31718_259-31719-237__"><span data-key="c559debe35fd4cc8b74a53aaa9f81e74"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="c559debe35fd4cc8b74a53aaa9f81e74:0">dir</code></span></span></a><span key="df51d592c08a4bab9fa8efc046748a7a"><span offset-key="df51d592c08a4bab9fa8efc046748a7a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="4d189fdc8fe948d2a6435d476b8069f3"><span offset-key="4d189fdc8fe948d2a6435d476b8069f3:0">Is exactly like "ls -C -b". (Files are by default listed in columns and sorted vertically.)</span></span>

### 

<span key="d8be0191f841484d862bb986083037d0"><span offset-key="d8be0191f841484d862bb986083037d0:0">Coreutils - Text Utilities</span></span>

List of coreutils text utilities

Text

<span key="62851712ca5b40dd864096fbdb73a4cd">**Command**</span>

<span key="4f7198673dae4a59b1b5684b63a419b9">**Description**</span>
